While the `GroupMetadataManagerTest` class (25907 lines) contains extensive tests, this analysis identifies **5+ critical failure modes** that are either untested or insufficiently tested. These gaps represent scenarios where group state transitions could fail silently or leave the group in an inconsistent state.\n\nThe primary risk areas are:\n1. **Partition assignment recovery after coordinator failover** - No explicit test for rebuilding target assignments when metadata is partially lost\n2. **Concurrent member operations during rebalance** - No test for race conditions between member removal and rebalance completion\n3. **Offset commit durability under rapid membership changes** - No test for offset durability guarantees when members are added/removed rapidly\n4. **Resource exhaustion with large topic subscriptions** - No test for graceful degradation when member count approaches `CONSUMER_GROUP_MAX_SIZE`\n5. **Regex subscription metadata refresh timeout** - No test for stale regex metadata causing inconsistent assignment\n6. **Epoch boundaries and wraparound** - No test for handling large epoch numbers near Integer.MAX_VALUE\n\n---\n\n## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Target Assignment Recovery Failure After Partial Metadata Loss\n\n**Risk**: HIGH\n\n**Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~lines 2415-2428 (updateTargetAssignment method)\n\n**Description**:\nWhen a coordinator restarts and reloads group metadata from `__consumer_offsets`, the `updateTargetAssignment()` method rebuilds the target assignment based on current subscriptions. If a consumer member's metadata record is corrupted or partially loaded, the assignor may receive incomplete member information, leading to:\n- Partitions being unassigned to any member\n- Duplicate partition assignments across members\n- Silent failures where the error is not propagated to clients\n\nThe current tests only verify happy-path assignment updates. There's no test simulating metadata load with missing or corrupted member subscription records.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testTargetAssignmentRecoveryWithCorruptedMemberMetadata() {\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    String memberId1 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    String memberId2 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    Uuid topicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n    String topicName = \"test-topic\";\n\n    CoordinatorMetadataImage metadataImage = new MetadataImageBuilder()\n        .addTopic(topicId, topicName, 6)\n        .addRacks()\n        .buildCoordinatorMetadataImage();\n\n    MockPartitionAssignor assignor = new MockPartitionAssignor(\"range\");\n    GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n        .withConfig(GroupCoordinatorConfig.CONSUMER_GROUP_ASSIGNORS_CONFIG, List.of(assignor))\n        .withMetadataImage(metadataImage)\n        .build();\n\n    // Simulate partial metadata load: member2 subscription missing\n    ConsumerGroupMember member1 = new ConsumerGroupMember.Builder(memberId1)\n        .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n        .setServerAssignorName(\"range\")\n        .setMemberEpoch(1)\n        .build();\n\n    // Replay only member1, skip member2's subscription record\n    context.replay(GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newConsumerGroupMemberSubscriptionRecord(groupId, member1));\n    context.replay(GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newConsumerGroupEpochRecord(groupId, 1, 0));\n\n    // Trigger rebalance by adding second member\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result = context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n        new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n            .setGroupId(groupId)\n            .setMemberId(memberId2)\n            .setMemberEpoch(0)\n            .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n            .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n            .setServerAssignor(\"range\")\n            .setTopicPartitions(List.of()));\n\n    // Assertion: Verify all partitions are assigned\n    assertNotNull(result.response());\n    assertTrue(result.records().stream().anyMatch(\n        record -> record instanceof ConsumerGroupTargetAssignmentMemberRecord\n    ), \"Target assignment must be generated\");\n\n    // Verify no partitions are left unassigned by checking that assignor receives both members\n    assignor.assertMembersInGroupAssignment(List.of(memberId1, memberId2));\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Tests the coordinator's resilience when metadata is incomplete during recovery\n- Exercises `updateTargetAssignment()` error handling path (~30 LOC)\n- Validates assignor receives correct member count for partition distribution\n- Covers metadata consistency checks after failover scenario\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Member Removal During Rebalance Target Assignment Update\n\n**Risk**: HIGH\n\n**Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~lines 4050-4100 (consumerGroupLeave and rebalance coordination)\n\n**Description**:\nWhen a member leaves during an active rebalance (while the group is computing or applying a new target assignment), the leave operation may:\n1. Remove the member record before target assignment is updated\n2. Fail to trigger a new rebalance round after member removal\n3. Leave the group in a state where remaining members never converge to a stable assignment because the new epoch is never computed\n\nThe test suite has `testUnknownGroupId()` and `testUnknownMemberIdJoinsConsumerGroup()` but lacks a test for the **race between member removal and active target assignment computation**.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testMemberRemovalDuringTargetAssignmentUpdate() {\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    String memberId1 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    String memberId2 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    Uuid topicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n    String topicName = \"test-topic\";\n\n    CoordinatorMetadataImage metadataImage = new MetadataImageBuilder()\n        .addTopic(topicId, topicName, 3)\n        .addRacks()\n        .buildCoordinatorMetadataImage();\n\n    long topicHash = computeTopicHash(topicName, metadataImage);\n\n    MockPartitionAssignor assignor = new .setClientId(DEFAULT_CLIENT_ID)\n        .setClientHost(DEFAULT_CLIENT_ADDRESS.toString())\n        .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n        .setServerAssignorName(\"range\")\n context.replay(GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newConsumerGroupTargetAssignmentEpochRecord(groupId, 100));\n         .setMemberId(memberId2)\n            .setMemberEpoch(0)\n            .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n            .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n pending rebalance state)\n    for (CoordinatorRecord record : join2.records()) {\n        context.replayRecord(record);\n    }\n\n    // **Critical Race**: Member1 leaves while group is in rebalance\n .setGroupId(groupId)\n            .setMemberId(memberId1)\n            .setMemberEpoch(-1)); // Leave with LEAVE_GROUP_MEMBER_EPOCH\n\n    assertEquals(Errors.NONE.code(), leave1.response().errorCode());\n\n    // Replay removal\n    for (CoordinatorRecord record : leave1.records()) {\n        context.replayRecord(record);\n    }\n\n    // Member2 should receive a new assignment without member1\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> hb2 = context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n        new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n            .setGroupId(groupId)\n            .setMemberId(memberId2)\n            .setMemberEpoch(1)\n            .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n            .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n            .setTopicPartitions(List.of()));\n\n    // Assertion: member2 must reach STABLE state and receive all partitions [0, 1, 2]\n    assertTrue(hb2.response().memberEpoch() > 1, \"Member epoch should advance after leave\");\n    assertNotNull(hb2.response().assignment(), \"Assignment must be provided\");\n\n    List<Integer> assignedPartitions = hb2.response().assignment().topicPartitions().stream()\n        .filter(tp -> tp.topicId().equals(topicId))\n        .flatMap(tp -> tp.partitions().stream())\n        .sorted()\n        .collect(Collectors.toList());\n    assertEquals(List.of(0, 1, 2), assignedPartitions, \"All partitions must be assigned to remaining member\");\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Tests `consumerGroupLeave()` interaction with active rebalance state (~70 LOC)\n- Validates `updateTargetAssignment()` is correctly triggered after member removal\n- Ensures epoch advancement happens correctly after concurrent leave/join\n- Covers the critical path where group consistency could be violated\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Offset Commit Loss During Rapid Membership Changes\n\n**Risk**: MEDIUM\n\n**Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~lines 5500-5700 (offset commit handling - not fully visible in read, but inferred from structure)\n\n**Description**:\nWhen a member joins/leaves rapidly, offset commit requests from that member may be processed against outdated group generation/member state. Specifically:\n1. A member commits offsets with generation G\n2. The group rebalances to generation G+1 before the commit is persisted\n3. The committed offset is lost or applied to the wrong generation\n\nWhile there are tests for `InvalidGenerationException` in classic groups, there's **no explicit test** for offset durability when consumer group members are added/removed during active commits.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testOffsetCommitDuringRapidMembershipChange() throws ExecutionException, LOC)\n- Validates offset durability guarantees\n- Exercises the intersection of `commitOffsets()` and rebalance state machine\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Consumer Group Max Size Enforcement Under Concurrent Joins\n\n**Risk**: MEDIUM\n\n**Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~lines 2318 (throwIfConsumerGroupIsFull call)\n\n**Description**:\nThe `throwIfConsumerGroupIsFull()` check at line 2318 prevents adding a member if the group size exceeds `consumerGroupMaxSize()`. However, if multiple members send join requests concurrently:\n1. Member A checks size: 99/100 → passes\n2. Member B checks size: 99/100 → passes\n3. Both get added → group now has 101 members, exceeding limit\n4. Subsequent requests fail due to group being \"full\"\n\nThere's **no test** that simulates this race condition by processing multiple overlapping join requests with tight group size boundaries.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testConsumerGroupMaxSizeEnforcementUnderConcurrentJoins() {\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    int maxGroupSize = 3; // Deliberately small for testing\n\n    MockPartitionAssignor assignor = new MockPartitionAssignor(\"range\");\n    GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n        .withConfig(GroupCoordinatorConfig.CONSUMER_GROUP_MAX_SIZE_CONFIG, maxGroupSize)\n        .withConfig(GroupCoordinatorConfig.CONSUMER_GROUP_ASSIGNORS_CONFIG, List.of(assignor))\n        .build();\n\n    List<String> memberIds = List.of(\n        Uuid.randomUuid().toString(),\n        Uuid.randomUuid().toString(),\n        Uuid.randomUuid().toString(),\n        Uuid.randomUuid().toString()  // One extra to trigger limit\n    );\n\n    int successCount = 0;\n    int rejectionCount = 0;\n\n    // Simulate 4 concurrent join requests (max size is 3)\n    for (String memberId : memberIds) {\n        try {\n            CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result =\n                context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n                    new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n                        .setGroupId(groupId)\n                        .setMemberId(memberId)\n                        .setMemberEpoch(0)\n                        .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n                        .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"test\"))\n                        .setServerAssignor(\"range\")\n                        .setTopicPartitions(List.of()));\n\n            if (result.response().errorCode() == Errors.NONE.code()) {\n                successCount++;\n                for (CoordinatorRecord record : result.records()) {\n                    context.replayRecord(record);\n                }\n            } else if (result.response().errorCode() == Errors.GROUP_MAX_SIZE_REACHED.code()) {\n                rejectionCount++;\n            } else {\n                fail(\"Unexpected error code: \" + result.response().errorCode());\n            }\n        } catch (GroupMaxSizeReachedException e) {\n            rejectionCount++;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Assertion: Exactly 3 members should succeed, 1 should be rejected\n    assertEquals(3, successCount, \"Exactly 3 members should be allowed to join\");\n    assertEquals(1, rejectionCount, \"Exactly 1 member should be rejected due to size limit\");\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Tests `throwIfConsumerGroupIsFull()` under concurrent load (~20 LOC)\n- Validates group size limits are enforced even with overlapping requests\n- Ensures `GroupMaxSizeReachedException` is properly thrown\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 5: Regex Subscription Metadata Refresh Timeout and Stale Metadata Assignment\n\n**Risk**: MEDIUM\n\n**Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~lines 2368-2374 (maybeUpdateRegularExpressions), ~lines 3400-3500 (regex resolution logic)\n\n**Description**:\nWhen a consumer member subscribes with a regex pattern (e.g., `test-.*`), the coordinator must resolve the regex to concrete topic names. If:\n1. A new topic matching the regex is created\n2. The metadata refresh deadline has not been reached (`hasMetadataExpired()`)\n3. The group is assigned an old topic set\n\nThen: **The new topic is never assigned to this member** until the refresh deadline expires. Current tests in `testConsumerHeartbeatRegexValidation()` only validate regex syntax, not stale metadata scenarios.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testRegexSubscriptionMetadataRefreshTimeout() {\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    String memberId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    Uuid oldTopicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n    Uuid newTopicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n    String oldTopicName = \"events-old\";\n    String newTopicName = \"events-new\";\n\n    // Initial metadata with only old topic\n    CoordinatorMetadataImage initialMetadata = new MetadataImageBuilder()\n        .addTopic(oldTopicId, oldTopicName, 1)\n        .addRacks()\n        .buildCoordinatorMetadataImage();\n\n    MockPartitionAssignor assignor = new MockPartitionAssignor(\"range\");\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(\n        new GroupAssignment(Map.of(memberId, new MemberAssignmentImpl(\n            Map.of(oldTopicId, List.of(0))\n        )))\n    );\n\n    GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n        .withConfig(GroupCoordinatorConfig.CONSUMER_GROUP_ASSIGNORS_CONFIG, List.of(assignor))\n        .withMetadataImage(initialMetadata)\n        .build();\n\n    // Member joins with regex subscription\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> join =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n            new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n                .setGroupId(groupId)\n                .setMemberId(memberId)\n While the `GroupMetadataManagerTest` class (25907 lines) contains extensive tests, this analysis identifies **5+ critical failure modes** that are either untested or insufficiently tested. These gaps represent scenarios where group state transitions could fail silently or leave the group in an inconsistent state.\n\nThe primary risk areas are:\n1. **Partition assignment recovery after coordinator failover** - No explicit test for rebuilding target assignments when metadata is partially lost\n2. **Concurrent member operations during rebalance** - No test for race conditions between member removal and rebalance completion\n3. **Offset commit durability under rapid membership changes** - No test for offset durability guarantees when members are added/removed rapidly\n4. **Resource exhaustion with large topic subscriptions** - No test for graceful degradation when member count approaches `CONSUMER_GROUP_MAX_SIZE`\n5. **Regex subscription metadata refresh timeout** - No test for stale regex metadata causing inconsistent assignment\n6. **Epoch boundaries and wraparound** - No test for handling large epoch numbers near Integer.MAX_VALUE\n\n---\n\n## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Target Assignment Recovery Failure After Partial Metadata Loss\n\n**Risk**: HIGH\n\n**Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~lines 2415-2428 (updateTargetAssignment method)\n\n**Description**:\nWhen a coordinator restarts and reloads group metadata from `__consumer_offsets`, the `updateTargetAssignment()` method rebuilds the target assignment based on current subscriptions. If a consumer member's metadata record is corrupted or partially loaded, the assignor may receive incomplete member information, leading to:\n- Partitions being unassigned to any member\n- Duplicate partition assignments across members\n- Silent failures where the error is not propagated to clients\n\nThe current tests only verify happy-path assignment updates. There's no test simulating metadata load with missing or corrupted member subscription records.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void .addTopic(topicId, topicName, 6)\n        .addRacks()\n        .buildCoordinatorMetadataImage();\n\n    MockPartitionAssignor assignor = new MockPartitionAssignor(\"range\");\n    GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n        .withConfig(GroupCoordinatorConfig.CONSUMER_GROUP_ASSIGNORS_CONFIG, List.of(assignor))\n        .withMetadataImage(metadataImage)\n        .build();\n\n    // Simulate partial metadata load: member2 subscription missing\n    ConsumerGroupMember member1 = new .setMemberEpoch(0)\n            .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n            .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n            .setServerAssignor(\"range\")\n            .setTopicPartitions(List.of()));\n\n    // Assertion: Verify all partitions are assigned\n    assertNotNull(result.response());\n    assertTrue(result.records().stream().anyMatch(\n        record -> and rebalance coordination)\n\n**Description**:\nWhen a member leaves during an active rebalance (while the group is computing or applying a new target assignment), the leave operation may:\n1. Remove the member record before target assignment is updated\n2. Fail to trigger a new rebalance round after member removal\n3. Leave the group in a state where remaining members never converge to a stable assignment because the new epoch is never computed\n\nThe test suite has `testUnknownGroupId()` and `testUnknownMemberIdJoinsConsumerGroup()` but lacks a test for the **race between member removal and active target assignment computation**.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testMemberRemovalDuringTargetAssignmentUpdate() {\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    String memberId1 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    String memberId2 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n .setGroupId(groupId)\n            .setMemberId(memberId1)\n            .setMemberEpoch(-1)); // Leave with LEAVE_GROUP_MEMBER_EPOCH\n\n    assertEquals(Errors.NONE.code(), leave1.response().errorCode());\n\n    // Replay removal\n    for (CoordinatorRecord record : leave1.records()) {\n        context.replayRecord(record);\n    }\n\n    // Member2 should receive a new     .setGroupId(groupId)\n            .setMemberId(memberId2)\n            .setMemberEpoch(1)\n            .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n            .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n            .setTopicPartitions(List.of()));\n\n    // Assertion: member2 must reach STABLE state and receive all partitions [0, 1, 2]\n    assertTrue(hb2.response().memberEpoch() > 1, \"Member epoch should advance after leave\");\n    assertNotNull(hb2.response().assignment(), \"Assignment must be provided\");\n\n    List<Integer> assignedPartitions = hb2.response().assignment().topicPartitions().stream()\n        .filter(tp -> tp.topicId().equals(topicId))\n        .flatMap(tp -> tp.partitions().stream())\n        .sorted()\n        .collect(Collectors.toList());\n    assertEquals(List.of(0, 1, 2), assignedPartitions, \"All partitions must be assigned to remaining member\");\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Tests `consumerGroupLeave()` interaction with active rebalance state (~70 LOC)\n- Validates `updateTargetAssignment()` is correctly triggered after member removal\n- Ensures epoch advancement happens correctly after concurrent leave/join\n- Covers the critical path where group consistency could be violated\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Offset Commit Loss During Rapid Membership Changes\n\n**Risk**: MEDIUM\n\n**Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~lines 5500-5700 (offset commit handling - not fully visible in read, but inferred from structure)\n\n**Description**:\nWhen a member joins/leaves rapidly, offset commit requests from that member may be processed against outdated group generation/member state. Specifically:\n1. A member commits offsets with generation G\n2. The group rebalances to generation G+1 before the commit is persisted\n3. The committed offset is lost or applied to the wrong generation\n\nWhile there are tests for `InvalidGenerationException` in classic groups, there's **no explicit test** for offset durability when consumer group members are added/removed during active commits.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testOffsetCommitDuringRapidMembershipChange() throws ExecutionException, Concurrent Joins\n\n**Risk**: MEDIUM\n\n**Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~lines 2318 (throwIfConsumerGroupIsFull call)\n\n**Description**:\nThe `throwIfConsumerGroupIsFull()` check at line 2318 prevents adding a member if the group size exceeds `consumerGroupMaxSize()`. However, if multiple members send join requests concurrently:\n1. Member A checks size: 99/100 → passes\n2. Member B checks size: 99/100 → passes\n3. Both get added → group now has 101 members, exceeding limit\n4. Subsequent requests fail due to group being \"full\"\n\nThere's **no test** that simulates this race condition by processing multiple overlapping join requests with tight group size boundaries.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testConsumerGroupMaxSizeEnforcementUnderConcurrentJoins() {\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    int maxGroupSize = 3; // Deliberately small for testing\n\n    MockPartitionAssignor assignor = new MockPartitionAssignor(\"range\");\n    GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n        .withConfig(GroupCoordinatorConfig.CONSUMER_GROUP_MAX_SIZE_CONFIG, maxGroupSize)\n        .withConfig(GroupCoordinatorConfig.CONSUMER_GROUP_ASSIGNORS_CONFIG, List.of(assignor))\n        .build();\n\n    List<String> memberIds = List.of(\n        Uuid.randomUuid().toString(),\n        Uuid.randomUuid().toString(),\n        Uuid.randomUuid().toString(),\n        Uuid.randomUuid().toString()  // One extra to trigger limit\n    );\n\n    int successCount = 0;\n    int rejectionCount = 0;\n\n    // Simulate 4 concurrent join requests (max size is 3)\n    for (String memberId : memberIds) {\n        try {\n            CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result =\n                context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n                    new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n                        .setGroupId(groupId)\n                        .setMemberId(memberId)\n                        .setMemberEpoch(0)\n                        .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n                        .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"test\"))\n                        .setServerAssignor(\"range\")\n                        .setTopicPartitions(List.of()));\n\n            if (result.response().errorCode() == Errors.NONE.code()) {\n                successCount++;\n                for (CoordinatorRecord record : result.records()) {\n                    context.replayRecord(record);\n                }\n            } else if (result.response().errorCode() == Errors.GROUP_MAX_SIZE_REACHED.code()) {\n                rejectionCount++;\n            } else {\n                fail(\"Unexpected error code: \" + result.response().errorCode());\n            }\n        } catch (GroupMaxSizeReachedException e) {\n            rejectionCount++;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Assertion: Exactly 3 members should succeed, 1 should be rejected\n    assertEquals(3, successCount, \"Exactly 3 members should be allowed to join\");\n    assertEquals(1, rejectionCount, \"Exactly 1 member should be rejected due to size limit\");\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Tests `throwIfConsumerGroupIsFull()` under concurrent load (~20 LOC)\n- Validates group size limits are enforced even with overlapping requests\n- Ensures `GroupMaxSizeReachedException` is properly thrown\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 5: Regex Subscription Metadata Refresh Timeout and Stale Metadata Assignment\n\n**Risk**: MEDIUM\n\n**Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~lines 2368-2374 (maybeUpdateRegularExpressions), ~lines 3400-3500 (regex resolution logic)\n\n**Description**:\nWhen a consumer member subscribes with a regex pattern (e.g., `test-.*`), the coordinator must resolve the regex to concrete topic names. If:\n1. A new topic matching the regex is created\n2. The metadata refresh deadline has not been reached (`hasMetadataExpired()`)\n3. The group is assigned an old topic set\n\nThen: **The new topic is never assigned to this member** until the refresh deadline expires. Current tests in `testConsumerHeartbeatRegexValidation()` only validate regex syntax, not stale metadata scenarios.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testRegexSubscriptionMetadataRefreshTimeout() {\n    String groupId = \"test-group\";\n    String memberId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    Uuid oldTopicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n    Uuid Wraparound and Integer.MAX_VALUE Boundary\n\n**Risk**: LOW (but HIGH impact if it occurs)\n\n**Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~lines 3200-3300 (member epoch increment logic)\n\n**Description**:\nMember epochs are incremented in a long-running cluster. While unlikely in practice, if a member's epoch reaches `Integer.MAX_VALUE` and wraps to negative:\n1. Subsequent epoch validation checks may incorrectly compare negative vs positive epochs\n2. Members may be incorrectly rejected as \"fenced\"\n3. The group becomes unable to process valid heartbeats\n\nThere's **no test** that simulates epoch wraparound or validates the epoch comparison logic near numeric boundaries.\n\n**Proposed .withMetadataImage(metadataImage)\n        .build();\n\n    // Create member with epoch near Integer.MAX_VALUE - 2\n    int epochNearMax = Integer.MAX_VALUE - 2;\n    ConsumerGroupMember member = new ConsumerGroupMember.Builder(memberId)\n        .setState(MemberState.STABLE)\n        .setMemberEpoch(epochNearMax)\n        .setPreviousMemberEpoch(epochNearMax - 1)\n        .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n        .setClientId(DEFAULT_CLIENT_ID)\n        .setClientHost(DEFAULT_CLIENT_ADDRESS.toString())\n        .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(topicName))\n        .setServerAssignorName(\"range\")\n        .setAssignedPartitions(mkAssignment(mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0)))\n        .build();\n\n    context.replay(GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newConsumerGroupMemberSubscriptionRecord(groupId, member));\n    context.replay(GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newConsumerGroupEpochRecord(groupId, epochNearMax,\n        computeGroupHash(Map.of(topicName, topicHash))));\n    context.replay(GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newConsumerGroupTargetAssignmentRecord(groupId, memberId,\n        mkAssignment(mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0))));\n    context.replay(GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newConsumerGroupTargetAssignmentEpochRecord(groupId, epochNearMax));\n    context.replay(GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newConsumerGroupCurrentAssignmentRecord(groupId, member));\n\n    // Send heartbeat with epoch at boundary (will be incremented)\n
